<s> footnote 89 sandy hook this waits upon you with the agreable news of our taking a spanish privateer on the 26th of septem'r last off of cape roman 90 att the no <\s>
<s> side of cuba who was conveying a brig'ne to the avanah which he had taken in the latitude 26 no <\s>
<s> coming from barbadoes bound to boston with rum sugar and some baggs of cotton <\s>
<s> we had the pleasure to meet him early in the morning and gave her chase <\s>
<s> when within a mile of her we hoisted our pennant <\s>
<s> she imediatly returned the compliment with her ensign att mast-head and a gunn to confirm it <\s>
<s> we received severall shott from her and chearfully return'd them <\s>
<s> then she made the best of her way crowding all the sail she cou'd and we doing the like came again within gun-shott and plyed her with our bow chase which were shifted to the fore ports for that purpose and she kept pelting of us with her stern chase out of her cabbin windows <\s>
<s> so that after severall brisk shott on both sides she struck <\s>
<s> our rigging mast and gunnell received some damage <\s>
<s> upwards of 25 shott went through our sails <\s>
<s> 2 shott went through our mast and in the weakest part just below where it was fisht <\s>
<s> a shott cut our fore shrewd 91 on the larboard side and another went through our starboard gunnell port and all <\s>
<s> we had only one man slightly wounded with a splinter by the enemy two others by an accident on board by one of the peoples peice going off after the engagement which shott them in the arm <\s>
<s> of the privateer was wounded in the arm and the bone fractured one negro boy killed and others wounded <\s>
<s> he was fitted out last novem'r att the avanah and went to st <\s>
<s> aug'ne and was on our coast early in the spring and took severall vessells as per list herein inclosed <\s>
<s> he was again fitted out in august last and had been on the coast again and had taken severall more vessells as you will observe by the acct but we had the good fortune to stop his cruize <\s>
<s> is name is don fransoiso loranzo and by all report tho an enemy a brave man endued with a great deal of clemensy and using his prisoners with a great deal of humanity <\s>
<s> the like usage he has on board for he justly deserves it <\s>

<s> our rigging mast and gunnell received some damage <\s>
<s> upwards of 25 shott went through our sails <\s>
<s> 2 shott went through our mast and in the weakest part just below where it was fisht <\s>
<s> a shott cut our fore shrewd 91 on the larboard side and another went through our starboard gunnell port and all <\s>
<s> we had only one man slightly wounded with a splinter by the enemy two others by an accident on board by one of the peoples peice going off after the engagement which shott them in the arm <\s>
<s> of the privateer was wounded in the arm and the bone fractured one negro boy killed and others wounded <\s>
<s> he was fitted out last novem'r att the avanah and went to st <\s>
<s> aug'ne and was on our coast early in the spring and took severall vessells as per list herein inclosed <\s>
<s> he was again fitted out in august last and had been on the coast again and had taken severall more vessells as you will observe by the acct but we had the good fortune to stop his cruize <\s>
<s> is name is don fransoiso loranzo and by all report tho an enemy a brave man endued with a great deal of clemensy and using his prisoners with a great deal of humanity <\s>
<s> the like usage he has on board for he justly deserves it <\s>
<s> footnote 90 an error of the quartermaster's in copying <\s>
<s> there is no cape roman on the north coast of cuba <\s>
<s> the captain had no doubt written cayo romano <\s>
<s> cayo romano is a small island one of the jardines del rey that fringe the north coast of eastern cuba bordering on the old bahama channel footnote 91 shroud we have sent you the sloop commanded by john webb loaded with sundry goods that has rec'd some damage which must desire you to unload directly and take care to gett them dryed <\s>
<s> there is also a negro boy that is sickly a negro man said to be taken off of barmudas by the privateer as he was a fishing and a mollatto belonging to some of the subjects or vassalls of the king of spain all which we recomend to your care that they may not elope <\s>
<s> the number of spanish prisoners taken on board is 48 out of which is eleven of the blood of negroes the capt <\s>
<s> included for which we dont doubt having his majestys bounty mony which is Â £ 5 ster <\s>
<s> we also desire that the vessell may not be condemned till our arrivall but only unloaded and a just acct <\s>
<s> taken of what on board <\s>
<s> as to the brigantine the capt <\s>
<s> of her whom we put in again out of civility has used us in a very rascally manner for he run away with the vessell from us in the night and no doubt with a design to cheat us of our salvage which is the one half of brig and cargo the enemy having had possession of her 22 days <\s>
<s> as she is a vessell of value hope you'l do your endeavours to recover our just dues and apply to the owners who are as we are credibly informed messrs <\s>
<s> lee and tyler of boston both under the state of conviction since the gospell of whitefield and tennant h as been propagated in new england 92 so that we are in hopes they will readily give a just acct <\s>
<s> of her cargo and her true value and render to caesar the things that are caesars which is the moral preachd by whitefield <\s>
<s> footnote 92 an allusion to the great awakening and to the revivalist preaching of george whitefield in boston in the autumn of 1740 and of gilbert tennent in the ensuing winter <\s>
<s> tyler at any rate john tyler of boxford and boston seems certainly to have been affected by the new light movement for in 1745 the second church in boxford suspended him among others for receiving into their houses itinerant preachers and holding meetings in opposition to the repeated entreaties of their brethren <\s>
<s> _the tyler genealogy i <\s>
<s> 43 as this will require a law suit i hope you'l gett the best advice you possibly can and gett her seized if att boston or else where and gett her condemned <\s>
<s> she was designed to be consign'd to you and the master sent on board to take possession and gett things in order to sail whilest we were getting letters wrote and bills of lading with a hand to go with him but he gave us the slip <\s>
<s> so relying on your care we don't doubt but you'll recover her and add her to the privateer prize <\s>
<s> the brig'ne was called the _sarah_ commanded by thos <\s>
<s> smith had on board 11 hhds <\s>
<s> of rum 23 hhds <\s>
<s> of sugar and 12 bags of cotton <\s>
<s> she was well fitted with 4 swivells one gun and other stores a new pink stern 93 vessell <\s>
<s> one of our hands he carryed with us 94 whose name is jerem'h harman who no doubt will acquaint you of the whole affair <\s>
<s> we hope you'l shew no favour to the capt <\s>
<s> for his ill usage and gett a just acct <\s>
<s> of his venture which one half is our due <\s>
<s> this affair is recomended to you by all the company and hope that you'll serve to the utmost of your powers not doubting in the least of your justice and equity <\s>

<s> footnote 89 sandy hook this waits upon you with the agreable news of our taking a spanish privateer on the 26th of septem'r last off of cape roman 90 att the no <\s>
<s> side of cuba who was conveying a brig'ne to the avanah which he had taken in the latitude 26 no <\s>
<s> coming from barbadoes bound to boston with rum sugar and some baggs of cotton <\s>
<s> we had the pleasure to meet him early in the morning and gave her chase <\s>
<s> when within a mile of her we hoisted our pennant <\s>
<s> she imediatly returned the compliment with her ensign att mast-head and a gunn to confirm it <\s>
<s> we received severall shott from her and chearfully return'd them <\s>

<s> for prison fees for a negro and mollo <\s>

<s> henry collins sent to mr <\s>
<s> steed evance who was desired to forward it to him <\s>

<s> thomas frankland whose first bill of exch'ge for Â £ 540 nec drawn by him on his brother messrs <\s>
<s> frankland and lightfoot merch's in boston togather with the amount of what we received for salvage for retaken that sloop was inclosed <\s>
<s> footnote 89 sandy hook this waits upon you with the agreable news of our taking a spanish privateer on the 26th of septem'r last off of cape roman 90 att the no <\s>
<s> side of cuba who was conveying a brig'ne to the avanah which he had taken in the latitude 26 no <\s>
<s> coming from barbadoes bound to boston with rum sugar and some baggs of cotton <\s>
<s> we had the pleasure to meet him early in the morning and gave her chase <\s>
<s> when within a mile of her we hoisted our pennant <\s>
<s> she imediatly returned the compliment with her ensign att mast-head and a gunn to confirm it <\s>
<s> we received severall shott from her and chearfully return'd them <\s>
<s> then she made the best of her way crowding all the sail she cou'd and we doing the like came again within gun-shott and plyed her with our bow chase which were shifted to the fore ports for that purpose and she kept pelting of us with her stern chase out of her cabbin windows <\s>
<s> so that after severall brisk shott on both sides she struck <\s>
<s> our rigging mast and gunnell received some damage <\s>
<s> upwards of 25 shott went through our sails <\s>
<s> 2 shott went through our mast and in the weakest part just below where it was fisht <\s>
<s> a shott cut our fore shrewd 91 on the larboard side and another went through our starboard gunnell port and all <\s>
<s> we had only one man slightly wounded with a splinter by the enemy two others by an accident on board by one of the peoples peice going off after the engagement which shott them in the arm <\s>
<s> of the privateer was wounded in the arm and the bone fractured one negro boy killed and others wounded <\s>
<s> he was fitted out last novem'r att the avanah and went to st <\s>
<s> aug'ne and was on our coast early in the spring and took severall vessells as per list herein inclosed <\s>
<s> he was again fitted out in august last and had been on the coast again and had taken severall more vessells as you will observe by the acct but we had the good fortune to stop his cruize <\s>
<s> is name is don fransoiso loranzo and by all report tho an enemy a brave man endued with a great deal of clemensy and using his prisoners with a great deal of humanity <\s>
<s> the like usage he has on board for he justly deserves it <\s>
<s> footnote 90 an error of the quartermaster's in copying <\s>
<s> there is no cape roman on the north coast of cuba <\s>
<s> the captain had no doubt written cayo romano <\s>
<s> cayo romano is a small island one of the jardines del rey that fringe the north coast of eastern cuba bordering on the old bahama channel footnote 91 shroud we have sent you the sloop commanded by john webb loaded with sundry goods that has rec'd some damage which must desire you to unload directly and take care to gett them dryed <\s>
<s> there is also a negro boy that is sickly a negro man said to be taken off of barmudas by the privateer as he was a fishing and a mollatto belonging to some of the subjects or vassalls of the king of spain all which we recomend to your care that they may not elope <\s>
<s> the number of spanish prisoners taken on board is 48 out of which is eleven of the blood of negroes the capt <\s>
<s> included for which we dont doubt having his majestys bounty mony which is Â £ 5 ster <\s>
<s> we also desire that the vessell may not be condemned till our arrivall but only unloaded and a just acct <\s>
<s> taken of what on board <\s>
<s> as to the brigantine the capt <\s>
<s> of her whom we put in again out of civility has used us in a very rascally manner for he run away with the vessell from us in the night and no doubt with a design to cheat us of our salvage which is the one half of brig and cargo the enemy having had possession of her 22 days <\s>
<s> as she is a vessell of value hope you'l do your endeavours to recover our just dues and apply to the owners who are as we are credibly informed messrs <\s>
<s> lee and tyler of boston both under the state of conviction since the gospell of whitefield and tennant h as been propagated in new england 92 so that we are in hopes they will readily give a just acct <\s>
<s> of her cargo and her true value and render to caesar the things that are caesars which is the moral preachd by whitefield <\s>
<s> footnote 92 an allusion to the great awakening and to the revivalist preaching of george whitefield in boston in the autumn of 1740 and of gilbert tennent in the ensuing winter <\s>
<s> tyler at any rate john tyler of boxford and boston seems certainly to have been affected by the new light movement for in 1745 the second church in boxford suspended him among others for receiving into their houses itinerant preachers and holding meetings in opposition to the repeated entreaties of their brethren <\s>
<s> _the tyler genealogy i <\s>
<s> 43 as this will require a law suit i hope you'l gett the best advice you possibly can and gett her seized if att boston or else where and gett her condemned <\s>
<s> she was designed to be consign'd to you and the master sent on board to take possession and gett things in order to sail whilest we were getting letters wrote and bills of lading with a hand to go with him but he gave us the slip <\s>
<s> so relying on your care we don't doubt but you'll recover her and add her to the privateer prize <\s>
<s> the brig'ne was called the _sarah_ commanded by thos <\s>
<s> smith had on board 11 hhds <\s>
<s> of rum 23 hhds <\s>
<s> of sugar and 12 bags of cotton <\s>
<s> she was well fitted with 4 swivells one gun and other stores a new pink stern 93 vessell <\s>
<s> one of our hands he carryed with us 94 whose name is jerem'h harman who no doubt will acquaint you of the whole affair <\s>
<s> we hope you'l shew no favour to the capt <\s>
<s> for his ill usage and gett a just acct <\s>
<s> of his venture which one half is our due <\s>
<s> this affair is recomended to you by all the company and hope that you'll serve to the utmost of your powers not doubting in the least of your justice and equity <\s>

<s> side of cuba and are in hopes of getting something worth while in a short time <\s>

<s> footnote 89 sandy hook this waits upon you with the agreable news of our taking a spanish privateer on the 26th of septem'r last off of cape roman 90 att the no <\s>
<s> side of cuba who was conveying a brig'ne to the avanah which he had taken in the latitude 26 no <\s>
<s> coming from barbadoes bound to boston with rum sugar and some baggs of cotton <\s>
<s> we had the pleasure to meet him early in the morning and gave her chase <\s>
<s> when within a mile of her we hoisted our pennant <\s>
<s> she imediatly returned the compliment with her ensign att mast-head and a gunn to confirm it <\s>
<s> we received severall shott from her and chearfully return'd them <\s>
<s> then she made the best of her way crowding all the sail she cou'd and we doing the like came again within gun-shott and plyed her with our bow chase which were shifted to the fore ports for that purpose and she kept pelting of us with her stern chase out of her cabbin windows <\s>
<s> so that after severall brisk shott on both sides she struck <\s>
<s> our rigging mast and gunnell received some damage <\s>
<s> upwards of 25 shott went through our sails <\s>
<s> 2 shott went through our mast and in the weakest part just below where it was fisht <\s>
<s> a shott cut our fore shrewd 91 on the larboard side and another went through our starboard gunnell port and all <\s>
<s> we had only one man slightly wounded with a splinter by the enemy two others by an accident on board by one of the peoples peice going off after the engagement which shott them in the arm <\s>
<s> of the privateer was wounded in the arm and the bone fractured one negro boy killed and others wounded <\s>
<s> he was fitted out last novem'r att the avanah and went to st <\s>
<s> aug'ne and was on our coast early in the spring and took severall vessells as per list herein inclosed <\s>
<s> he was again fitted out in august last and had been on the coast again and had taken severall more vessells as you will observe by the acct but we had the good fortune to stop his cruize <\s>
<s> is name is don fransoiso loranzo and by all report tho an enemy a brave man endued with a great deal of clemensy and using his prisoners with a great deal of humanity <\s>
<s> the like usage he has on board for he justly deserves it <\s>
<s> footnote 90 an error of the quartermaster's in copying <\s>
<s> there is no cape roman on the north coast of cuba <\s>
<s> the captain had no doubt written cayo romano <\s>
<s> cayo romano is a small island one of the jardines del rey that fringe the north coast of eastern cuba bordering on the old bahama channel footnote 91 shroud we have sent you the sloop commanded by john webb loaded with sundry goods that has rec'd some damage which must desire you to unload directly and take care to gett them dryed <\s>
<s> there is also a negro boy that is sickly a negro man said to be taken off of barmudas by the privateer as he was a fishing and a mollatto belonging to some of the subjects or vassalls of the king of spain all which we recomend to your care that they may not elope <\s>
<s> the number of spanish prisoners taken on board is 48 out of which is eleven of the blood of negroes the capt <\s>
<s> included for which we dont doubt having his majestys bounty mony which is Â £ 5 ster <\s>
<s> we also desire that the vessell may not be condemned till our arrivall but only unloaded and a just acct <\s>
<s> taken of what on board <\s>
<s> as to the brigantine the capt <\s>
<s> of her whom we put in again out of civility has used us in a very rascally manner for he run away with the vessell from us in the night and no doubt with a design to cheat us of our salvage which is the one half of brig and cargo the enemy having had possession of her 22 days <\s>
<s> as she is a vessell of value hope you'l do your endeavours to recover our just dues and apply to the owners who are as we are credibly informed messrs <\s>
<s> lee and tyler of boston both under the state of conviction since the gospell of whitefield and tennant h as been propagated in new england 92 so that we are in hopes they will readily give a just acct <\s>
<s> of her cargo and her true value and render to caesar the things that are caesars which is the moral preachd by whitefield <\s>
<s> footnote 92 an allusion to the great awakening and to the revivalist preaching of george whitefield in boston in the autumn of 1740 and of gilbert tennent in the ensuing winter <\s>
<s> tyler at any rate john tyler of boxford and boston seems certainly to have been affected by the new light movement for in 1745 the second church in boxford suspended him among others for receiving into their houses itinerant preachers and holding meetings in opposition to the repeated entreaties of their brethren <\s>
<s> _the tyler genealogy i <\s>
<s> 43 as this will require a law suit i hope you'l gett the best advice you possibly can and gett her seized if att boston or else where and gett her condemned <\s>
<s> she was designed to be consign'd to you and the master sent on board to take possession and gett things in order to sail whilest we were getting letters wrote and bills of lading with a hand to go with him but he gave us the slip <\s>
<s> so relying on your care we don't doubt but you'll recover her and add her to the privateer prize <\s>
<s> the brig'ne was called the _sarah_ commanded by thos <\s>
<s> smith had on board 11 hhds <\s>
<s> of rum 23 hhds <\s>
<s> of sugar and 12 bags of cotton <\s>
<s> she was well fitted with 4 swivells one gun and other stores a new pink stern 93 vessell <\s>
<s> one of our hands he carryed with us 94 whose name is jerem'h harman who no doubt will acquaint you of the whole affair <\s>
<s> we hope you'l shew no favour to the capt <\s>
<s> for his ill usage and gett a just acct <\s>
<s> of his venture which one half is our due <\s>
<s> this affair is recomended to you by all the company and hope that you'll serve to the utmost of your powers not doubting in the least of your justice and equity <\s>

<s> side of cuba and are in hopes of getting something worth while in a short time <\s>

<s> for his ill usage and gett a just acct <\s>
<s> of his venture which one half is our due <\s>

<s> footnote 89 sandy hook this waits upon you with the agreable news of our taking a spanish privateer on the 26th of septem'r last off of cape roman 90 att the no <\s>
<s> side of cuba who was conveying a brig'ne to the avanah which he had taken in the latitude 26 no <\s>
<s> coming from barbadoes bound to boston with rum sugar and some baggs of cotton <\s>
<s> we had the pleasure to meet him early in the morning and gave her chase <\s>
<s> when within a mile of her we hoisted our pennant <\s>
<s> she imediatly returned the compliment with her ensign att mast-head and a gunn to confirm it <\s>
<s> we received severall shott from her and chearfully return'd them <\s>
<s> then she made the best of her way crowding all the sail she cou'd and we doing the like came again within gun-shott and plyed her with our bow chase which were shifted to the fore ports for that purpose and she kept pelting of us with her stern chase out of her cabbin windows <\s>
<s> so that after severall brisk shott on both sides she struck <\s>
<s> our rigging mast and gunnell received some damage <\s>
<s> upwards of 25 shott went through our sails <\s>
<s> 2 shott went through our mast and in the weakest part just below where it was fisht <\s>
<s> a shott cut our fore shrewd 91 on the larboard side and another went through our starboard gunnell port and all <\s>
<s> we had only one man slightly wounded with a splinter by the enemy two others by an accident on board by one of the peoples peice going off after the engagement which shott them in the arm <\s>
<s> of the privateer was wounded in the arm and the bone fractured one negro boy killed and others wounded <\s>
<s> he was fitted out last novem'r att the avanah and went to st <\s>
<s> aug'ne and was on our coast early in the spring and took severall vessells as per list herein inclosed <\s>
<s> he was again fitted out in august last and had been on the coast again and had taken severall more vessells as you will observe by the acct but we had the good fortune to stop his cruize <\s>
<s> is name is don fransoiso loranzo and by all report tho an enemy a brave man endued with a great deal of clemensy and using his prisoners with a great deal of humanity <\s>
<s> the like usage he has on board for he justly deserves it <\s>
<s> footnote 90 an error of the quartermaster's in copying <\s>
<s> there is no cape roman on the north coast of cuba <\s>
<s> the captain had no doubt written cayo romano <\s>
<s> cayo romano is a small island one of the jardines del rey that fringe the north coast of eastern cuba bordering on the old bahama channel footnote 91 shroud we have sent you the sloop commanded by john webb loaded with sundry goods that has rec'd some damage which must desire you to unload directly and take care to gett them dryed <\s>
<s> there is also a negro boy that is sickly a negro man said to be taken off of barmudas by the privateer as he was a fishing and a mollatto belonging to some of the subjects or vassalls of the king of spain all which we recomend to your care that they may not elope <\s>
<s> the number of spanish prisoners taken on board is 48 out of which is eleven of the blood of negroes the capt <\s>
<s> included for which we dont doubt having his majestys bounty mony which is Â £ 5 ster <\s>
<s> we also desire that the vessell may not be condemned till our arrivall but only unloaded and a just acct <\s>
<s> taken of what on board <\s>
<s> as to the brigantine the capt <\s>
<s> of her whom we put in again out of civility has used us in a very rascally manner for he run away with the vessell from us in the night and no doubt with a design to cheat us of our salvage which is the one half of brig and cargo the enemy having had possession of her 22 days <\s>
<s> as she is a vessell of value hope you'l do your endeavours to recover our just dues and apply to the owners who are as we are credibly informed messrs <\s>
<s> lee and tyler of boston both under the state of conviction since the gospell of whitefield and tennant h as been propagated in new england 92 so that we are in hopes they will readily give a just acct <\s>
<s> of her cargo and her true value and render to caesar the things that are caesars which is the moral preachd by whitefield <\s>
<s> footnote 92 an allusion to the great awakening and to the revivalist preaching of george whitefield in boston in the autumn of 1740 and of gilbert tennent in the ensuing winter <\s>
<s> tyler at any rate john tyler of boxford and boston seems certainly to have been affected by the new light movement for in 1745 the second church in boxford suspended him among others for receiving into their houses itinerant preachers and holding meetings in opposition to the repeated entreaties of their brethren <\s>
